<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vakkundig.html>vakkundig</a> (32208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vak.html>vak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">occupation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kundig.html>kundig</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">capable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***vakwerk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vakwerk.html>vakwerk</a> (22066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vak.html>vak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">section, compartment; business, trade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">work</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The sense “timber framing” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> likely derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fachwerk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vakwerk.html>vakwerk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vakwerk.html>vakwerken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vakwerk.html>vakwerkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A good, <span class="Latn" lang="en">professional</span>-level <span class="Latn" lang="en">job</span>, ably skilled performance.</li>
<li>A construction technique where a building's (exterior) <span class="Latn" lang="en">wall</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> divided up by wooden <span class="Latn" lang="en">lath</span>s into <a href = vnd.unilang:squares.html>squares</a>, often subdivided diagonally, then each square or triangle filled up with plaster etc.; a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/timber_framing" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:timber framing">timber-framing</a> construction. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li>A truss, a support structure of interconnected beams or girders forming triangles. <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vakbekwaam</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vakman.html>vakman</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meesterwerk.html>meesterwerk</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pleisterwerk.html>pleisterwerk</a></span></li></ul>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evening</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>nightfall, <a href = vnd.unilang:sundown.html>sundown</a>, dusk

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">valke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:falco.html>falco</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*falkō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*falkô</i>.

***vals.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vals.html>vals</a> (2252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">valsch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fals</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">falsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vals.html>vals</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:valser.html>valser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vals.html>vals</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">valst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fake, false

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> off-key, out of tune
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zuiver.html>zuiver</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>vicious
<ul><li><b>1619</b>, Hendrick Slatius, <i>Ioannes Calvinus, <a href = vnd.unilang:vreden.html>vreedt</a>, bitter, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vals.html>vals</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>: Corte ende cleare verbeldinghe <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den aert oft gheest Ioannis Calvini ... <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>Eerst</a> gheteeckent <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> eenen <a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebber</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Nederlantsche [i.e. H. Slatius], etc</i></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> incorrect, untrue</li></ol>

***van.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> (12)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fanē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pone</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pana</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*apo-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pā-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">off, of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fana</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">fan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">fon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fona</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></strong>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fanôf</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vangen.html>vangen</a> (1726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vangen.html>vangen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fangan</i>. Back-formed from the past-tense forms of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fān</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fanhaną</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>tonight, this night, the night at the end of the current day
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vannacht.html>Vannacht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zul.html>zul</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slapen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You’<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> sleep well <b>tonight</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>last night, the night at the end if the previous day
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vannacht.html>Vannacht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslapen.html>geslapen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> sleep well <b>last night</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>As in the example sentences, the distinction between the two meanings <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> through the tense of the verb (past versus non-past). When both the last and the coming <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>nights</a> are mentioned, however, the former will be referred to with the synonym <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gisternacht</i>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nacht.html>nacht</a></i> may also be used for the coming night: <i>Gisternacht <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslapen.html>geslapen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nacht.html>nacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeker.html>zeker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>.</i> (“Last night I didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> sleep well, but this night I surely will.”)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">last night</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">gisternacht</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>self-evident, evidently, obviously</li>
<li>(to be) <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> for granted, naturally</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> vapour</h1><br><a href = vnd.unilang:stoom.html>stoom</a><br>damp<br><a href = vnd.unilang:wasem.html>wasem</a><br></body> 
***varen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:varen.html>varen</a> (3119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vāren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">faran</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faraną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varen.html>varen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To sail; to go by boat; to navigate</li>
<li>To ascend or descend</li>
<li>To fare</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the official "<a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>Groene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boekje.html>Boekje</a>" (the legal spelling standard for Dutch), the past tense for most senses <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> strong. Only the sense “to fare” <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a weak past tense form.
</p><p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">most senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> Strong conjugation.
</p>

<p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to fare</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> Mixed conjugation.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:varen.html>varen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*farn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*farną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varen.html>varen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varens.html>varens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varentje.html>varentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fern, plant of the class Polypodiopsida</li></ol>

***varken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:varken.html>varken</a> (2377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:varken.html>varken</a></i>. Equivalent to an old diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">var</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*farhaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language">Central Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">Ferke</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varken.html>varken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varkens.html>varkens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varkentje.html>varkentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeug.html>zeug</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pig, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sus_scrofa_domesticus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Sus scrofa domesticus"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:sus.html>Sus</a> scrofa domesticus</i></a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A swine, a dirty, gross or foul person.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> possibly  offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A student who does not belong to a student society; one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> neither a frat boy nor a soror.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knor.html>knor</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A brush, especially one used along with a dustpan for sweeping floors or hearths.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borstel.html>borstel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schuier</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***vast.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a> (184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fast</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fastuz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaster.html>vaster</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vastst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>firm, fast, tight</li>
<li>fixed, not moving or changing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vaste.html>vaste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lasten.html>lasten</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>fixed</b> costs</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stuck, unable to get out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in the solid state</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> perennial</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a telephone</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> using a landline</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>surely, certainly

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sarcastically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sure, yeah, right
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> at <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huiswerk.html>huiswerk</a>.<i>  |  </i><a href = vnd.unilang:ja.html>Ja</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My dog <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> my homework.  |  <b>Yeah, right</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vasten.html>vasten</a> (17944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vasten.html>vasten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*faston</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fastāną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vasten.html>vasten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to fast</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vastene</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fastunna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fastubniją</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fastubnijō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fastunnia</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍆𐌰𐍃𐍄𐌿𐌱𐌽𐌹</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fastubni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vasten.html>vasten</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>fast (period of time when one abstains from or eats very little food)</li></ol>
